Women's Paradise

Obesity and Women's Aesthetic Sense 195

— Bingyu

Modern women are often troubled by being overweight, which not only reduces the beauty of their appearance, but also makes their hearts and breathing very uncomfortable due to their obesity. Other related problems such as arteriosclerosis and high blood pressure also occur. At worst, they suddenly suffer from dangerous diseases such as heart paralysis and cerebral hemorrhage, and even suffer from pulmonary tuberculosis, resulting in death. Also, due to obesity, the reproductive organs are obstructed, the liver becomes abnormal, and secondary diseases such as neuritis and diabetes will continue to occur. Although obese people have relatively few germs, once an infectious disease occurs, it is easier to spread than in thin people. Therefore, the mortality rate of obese people worldwide is higher than that of thin people. Ordinary physiques absorb fat in April and May, and gradually become thinner in summer. If obese people eat too much fatty food in winter, the amount of fat increases, and they suffer even more in summer. Moreover, because of obesity, the original aesthetic sense is taken away, especially for young women, which must be paid great attention to. Recently, the number of obese women in the leisure class in Europe and the United States has increased year by year. Now the fat center theory has been invented. This disease is more common in Chinese women than in Europeans and Americans, because they often eat starchy top-grade rice, and their fat gradually increases. Therefore, obese women must not eat too much food containing too much fat during the season when their appetite increases in winter, such as meat, refined rice, and foods with too much oil. That can inhibit the development of the thyroid gland, because obese people do not eat much fatty food in winter, and the development principle of body metabolism can gradually flourish in the following spring and summer without being hindered. In particular, pay attention to exercise to reduce excess fat and revitalize its development function, so that the feeling of height and weight gradually becomes balanced, which is really an essential element to promote health and beauty.

How Thin Women Can Get Fat 196

— Chuyu

It is true that women's bodies that are too obese reduce their sense of beauty, but it is also unsightly to be as thin as a stick. Now I have brought out the experimental fattening method, please try it out with thin women. (1) Chicken bone soup is good for thinness. Use a chicken bone frame every day, which must have the bones of the whole body, and boil it into soup with green vegetables (simmer it with a simmer until the bones are crispy), add a little salt, and drink it three times. It is very delicious and very nourishing. If you continue to eat it for half a month, you will only eat fifteen chickens, which will cost you less than ten yuan, and it can prove to be effective. If you can get Silkie chickens, it will be even more effective, but your mind and body must be quiet, and you must not be irritable, and then add appropriate exercise, then your body will achieve considerable health and beauty. (2) Binding the abdomen to make you fat. Women who are generally willow-like often suffer from neurasthenia, indigestion, constipation, insomnia and other symptoms. If you want to get fat, you can use a cloth six feet long and five inches wide and tie it tightly to the lower abdomen (below the navel), tie the head to the left, and distribute the posture evenly according to the traction when exercising. Eat more beans, noodles, brown rice, etc. every day, and sit quietly in a balanced posture for ten minutes before going to bed. Then the body will not be harmful if it is too much or insufficient, and you can gradually become healthier. (3) Drinking water and dry cloth friction method. Drink a cup of clear water on an empty stomach every morning, drink two cups at ten o'clock in the morning, drink a cup before lunch, drink two cups at three o'clock in the afternoon, and drink a cup before dinner. The amount and time of drinking every day must be fixed and not early or late. At the same time, rub the whole body twice with a dry cloth when you get up and before going to bed every day. Start rubbing from the back first, then rub the chest, abdomen, hands and feet, until the skin is red. You will get fat in less than a month. (4) Food nutrition and mental life method. Food can absorb nutrients, such as yams, vegetables, noodles, beans, chicken eggs, milk, fish, etc. You must take a certain amount every day, and eat animal meat once every other day. You must not eat too much or too little, and you must have a fixed time. For mental treatment, the first is to keep the mind quiet. The second is to have proper rules in daily life. The third is to fully absorb fresh air. The fourth is to avoid excessive exercise. If you do this, not only ordinary people can increase their health and beauty, but also people with lung disease can be treated. The above four methods are all from experiments, so thin women may wish to try it.

Current Situation of Education in Anhui Province (II) 201

| Inspection Report by Special Commissioner Li Ximou of the Ministry of Education |

(5) The Current Situation of Local Education Funds and Opinions on the Reorganization Plan: After the flood in the 20th year of the Republic of China, the disaster areas suffered losses. Counties such as Liu'an and Huoshan were also ravaged by bandits, leading to economic bankruptcy and severe damage to education funds. The Department of Education compiled "Statistics on County Education Revenue for the 21st Year of the Republic of China," covering the education funds of 59 counties: (1) School property rent income: 485,912 yuan; (2) Local produce education tax: 134,253 yuan; (3) Various surcharges: 771,596 yuan; (4) Free education surcharge: 771,260 yuan; (5) Subsidies and donations: 33,453 yuan; (6) Miscellaneous items: 77,796 yuan; (7) Temporary income: 473,946 yuan. The total of the above seven items is 2,748,216 yuan. "Statistics on County Education Expenditure for the 21st Year of the Republic of China" show that the education funds of various counties are spent on: (1) Secondary education: 240,539 yuan; (2) Primary education: 973,700 yuan; (3) Vocational education: 365,276 yuan; (4) Subsidies: 10,492 yuan; (5) Social education: 179,058 yuan; (6) Education Bureau expenses:

228,454 yuan; (7) Expenses for various school districts and committees: 45,182 yuan; (8) Miscellaneous expenses: 69,975 yuan; (9) Various temporary expenses: 613,291 yuan. The total of the above nine items is 2,725,976 yuan. In various counties, most of the surcharges are collected on behalf of the county government and other agencies, while school property rents are collected by people sent by the Education Bureau. According to the Fengyang County Education Bureau's report on income and expenditure, "The county education funds collected on behalf of the county government and other agencies are settled monthly by the Education Bureau. The four-part receipt form issued by the Department is used to collect funds. The Education Bureau collects school rents itself, with one director and one collector of school property management handling the matter. Collection and payment are done simultaneously, and the accounting staff of the Bureau settles accounts at the end of the month, filling out the four-part receipt form issued by the Department. As for the disbursement method, at the end of each month, the total amount of funds collected that month is calculated, and free school expenses are prioritized. The remainder is distributed proportionally to general schools and various educational institutions. When receiving funds, a four-part disbursement receipt form issued by the Department must be filled out for reference. A budget is prepared at the beginning of the year as a standard for income and expenditure. At the end of the year, a final account is prepared to serve as a statistic for assessing profit and loss. The actual monthly income and expenditure are calculated monthly and submitted to the county for verification and then forwarded to the Department for record." There are also several difficulties, such as the Fengyang Education Bureau stating, "There are two difficulties in the Education Bureau's management of education funds: (1) County governments inevitably misappropriate funds collected on their behalf. Although the province has repeatedly issued strict orders to remit funds as soon as they are collected without any misappropriation, the effect is still minimal. It is estimated that the five county magistrates, Jiang, Luo, Zhang, Yang, and Shi, have misappropriated a total of 7,900 yuan. Former County Magistrate Yuan also misappropriated more than 1,600 yuan. Although they are all listed as offsets, and the province has ordered that they be recovered and reimbursed from various taxes, there are no concrete measures, and reimbursement remains empty words. (2) Many school properties have been affected by floods, resulting in reduced income, and monthly expenditures are insufficient. Therefore, general education funds can only be distributed proportionally, which is very difficult. (3) Many school properties have not been properly registered by the Education Bureau, and procedures are incomplete, causing property rights to be unstable." The Huaining County Education Bureau stated, "The county education funds come from four items: additional land tax, additional house rent, school rent, and fishing lake and shoal tax. The estimated regular income for this year is 43,486 yuan, but the actual income is likely to be only over 30,000 yuan. This is because rice prices have fallen in recent years, the rural economy has collapsed, and the additional land tax cannot be fully collected. The Education Bureau's school rent is also no exception. In addition, for house rent, most of the residents are from this county and have been living here for a long time, making it inconvenient to increase rents for the time being. As for the fishing lake and shoal tax, the income from the past two years of major floods has only been enough to meet the needs of building embankments, resulting in a shortage of overall education fund income, making it impossible for all educational undertakings to proceed smoothly, which is truly regrettable." Therefore, in order to ensure that local education funds meet the standards of the Ministry of Education, it is necessary to increase revenue and ensure its independence so that local compulsory education and social education can be gradually promoted. It seems that there is a need to reorganize local education funds, and the reorganization methods must be adapted to local conditions. The Anhui Department of Education's tentatively drafted reorganization measures and plans for local education funds are recorded below: (A) "Measures for Reorganizing Local Education Funds": This year's provincial supervisors in Anhui Province are inspecting local education in various counties slightly differently from previous years. In the entire province, in addition to the provincial capital's public and private primary and secondary schools and social education institutions being inspected jointly or in groups by various supervisors, four counties, Liu'an, Huoqiu, Huoshan, and Lihuang, are assigned special commissioners for reorganization. Inspection is divided into five inspection zones, with each zone inspecting for one year. The supervisors designated in each zone, in addition to inspection, pay special attention to guidance work. Regarding the reorganization of local education funds, the following items are included: (1) The allocation standards for education funds in various counties should be implemented in accordance with the orders of the Department. Temporary income can only be used for temporary expenses. If there is a percentage of income, a special report should be submitted to the Department for approval before it can be used. (2) When preparing the budget, Education Bureaus in various counties are absolutely not allowed to falsely list income or inflate expenses. At the end of each month, income and expenditure reports for the month should be prepared separately according to the nature of the funds and submitted to the Department for record. (3) County governments and financial institutions in various counties are not allowed to misappropriate or divert education surcharges collected on their behalf. They should be handed over to the Education Bureau for safekeeping as soon as they are collected, and a settlement should be made jointly at the end of each month. (4) School properties in various counties should be registered comprehensively within a limited time and reported to the Department for record. (5) Education Bureaus in various counties should allocate funds sparingly according to the budget and should not arbitrarily misuse them or delay reporting expenses. (6) School rents in various counties should be collected directly from tenants by the Education Bureau, and any dual systems should be abolished. (7) Special funds for free education in various counties should be used exclusively for compulsory education and should not be diverted to other uses. (8) After clearing the expenses for the current month, Education Bureaus in various counties should prepare cash disbursement calculations and bureau expenditure statements, etc., according to the receipt and expenditure report form and the amount disbursed, and submit them to the Department for verification. (9) After the cash disbursement calculations and bureau expenditure statements, etc., for previous months have been verified by the Department, the income and expenditure final accounts for the previous year should be prepared and submitted to the Department for review. (10) Expenses outside the budget that have not been approved by the Department should be compensated by the Bureau Chief personally. (11) Education Bureaus in various counties should recover special funds for vocational education within a limited time and deposit them in banks or reputable shops. Private storage is strictly prohibited. (B) "Plan for Reorganizing Local Education Funds": The Anhui Provincial Department of Education's plan for reorganizing local education funds is roughly divided into two parts: (1) Investigation and Clearance of School Funds: Based on the economic situation in Anhui Province in recent years, it is not reasonable or permissible to actively increase revenue and increase the burden on the people. The Provincial Department of Education now plans to thoroughly investigate the special funds that have been designated in order to clarify the actual situation. For the actual monthly income and expenditure of each county Education Bureau, a monthly income and expenditure report form should be filled out and submitted within a limited time. A detailed investigation should be made of the total amount of free and general education funds accumulated in each county, the situation of occupation or misappropriation by other agencies, and the current storage status, and each should be thoroughly reorganized and recovered separately, and properly stored by the county Education Bureaus. (2) Reorganization of School Properties: Regarding school properties in various counties, the Department plans to conduct a general registration of all school fields, houses, rents, and taxes in various counties. After the registration is completed, the Provincial Government will be requested to send personnel to various counties to conduct on-site measurement and reorganization to see if there is any encroachment or profiteering, or underreporting of income. After the special commissioners have clearly reorganized the school properties in each county, they will separately draw up diagrams and submit them to the Department for reference. The Department will then request the Provincial Government to restrict the arbitrary sale of school properties by various counties. (6) Implementation Status of the First Phase of Compulsory Education and Short-Term Vocational Education in Mass Schools: The implementation of mass schools and compulsory education has not yet achieved significant results. The biggest difficulties are approximately two: (1) It is not easy to raise funds. (2) It is difficult to recruit teachers and talent. In addition, most of the current mass education personnel are accommodating to the status quo and lack the spirit of improvement, so the results are not significant. The first phase of compulsory education, originally set from August of the 21st year to July of the 24th year, has not yet begun in Anhui Province, likely due to the two difficult problems of economy and teachers. A first-phase compulsory education implementation plan is currently being drafted, ordering all departments to follow it in preparing for the establishment of compulsory education pilot zones in urban and rural areas of each county, and setting a deadline for them to formulate plans and maps based on the conditions of each county and submit them to the Department for record.

Regarding short-term vocational education, the Provincial Department of Education has drafted an implementation plan, ordering various counties to organize it within a limited time. Currently, the counties that have submitted plans include Taihu, He County, Langxi, Hao County, Huaining, Nanling, Taiping, Guichi, Susong, Mengcheng, Jixi, Dingyuan, Fengyang, Zhide, and Tianchang, a total of fifteen counties. All have been reviewed by the Department and ordered to actively proceed from the second semester of this year. The remaining counties have also recently submitted plans one after another. In the future, in addition to ordering various counties to report the progress of the work to the Department for record at any time, the Department also ordered the provincial supervisors in each zone to earnestly supervise and promote the plans formulated by various counties, with the goal of ensuring that all out-of-school children of appropriate age in various places receive the minimum level of education within five years.

A model zone for free education is being prepared. Currently, it is planned to first establish two compulsory education and short-term compulsory education pilot zones in urban and rural areas of Huaining County, the location of the provincial capital, as models for promoting free education in various counties. In terms of funding, more than 10,000 yuan has been raised. A preparatory committee is currently being organized and plans to begin investigating schools, school-age children, out-of-school children of appropriate age, children in school, and private tutoring, temples, and ancestral halls, etc., in urban and rural areas near the provincial capital. Once the investigation is completed, the Department plans to make practical preparations based on the actual local conditions.

(To be continued)

Education Plan for Guangdong Province in the 23rd Year of the Republic 202

Admit a Minimum of One-Half of Out-of-School Children in All Counties and Cities

Increase Funding for Vocational Education and Promote Mass Military Education

Guangdong's educational administration has been implemented in accordance with the Guangdong Three-Year Administrative Plan in recent years. This year, the entire province's educational construction plan for the 23rd year of the Republic is still based on the administrative plan. The Department of Education has recently drafted it and will implement it step by step. The outline of the plan is as follows: (1) Improve education at all levels of schools: 1. Increase education funding and ensure its independence; 2. Ensure the protection of education personnel; 3. Assess the performance of education administrators and reward and punish them accordingly; 4. Reward diligent students and assess their academic performance and conduct; 5. Assess the implementation of the Three Principles of the People education plan and make practical revisions; (2) Compulsory education: 1. Continue to increase the number of primary schools and classes, with the goal of admitting a minimum of one-half of out-of-school children in all counties and cities; (3) Secondary education: 1. Increase the number of provincial secondary school classes; (4) Vocational education: 1. Increase the number of vocational schools; 2. All provincial schools should add advanced vocational classes; 3. All county and municipal schools should attach junior vocational classes; 4. Supervise counties and cities to increase funding for vocational education; 5. Prepare for the establishment of vocational supplementary schools and increase the number of supplementary classes; (5) Teacher training: 1. Actively promote kindergarten education; 2. Implement various regulations for the service of normal school graduates; 3. Quantitative expansion of normal schools in counties and cities; 4. Investigate and collect statistics on the status of normal education throughout the province and the qualifications of primary and secondary school teachers; 5. Continue the registration of normal school graduates; (6) Social education: 1. Expand the operations of the Provincial Experimental Mass Education Center; 2. Counties and cities begin to train social education personnel; 3. Prepare for the establishment of county, city, district, and township mass education centers or farmer education centers; 4. Establish a social education college and encourage universities in this province to add departments of sociology; 5. Organize cooperative workshops; 6. Promote the experimental zone system for social education; 7. Increase the number of mass schools, with each senior primary school in the province attaching a mass school; 8. Expand the literacy movement; 9. Expand the sports experimental zone and develop national physical education; 10. Promote mass military education; (7) Higher education: 1. Lingnan University's College of Engineering will add a department of agricultural product manufacturing and a department of electrical engineering; 2. Establish a Lingnan University School of Commerce; 3. Continue to subsidize private universities in the province and supervise their improvement; 4. Continue to send students to study abroad; 5. Establish a provincial agricultural vocational school; 6. Establish an instrument manufacturing institute; (8) Military training: 1. Complete the second round of military training for all high schools and above in the province; 2. Hold military competitions for high schools and above throughout the province; (9) Local education administration: 1. Establish a training institute for local education administrators.

High School Students in Anhui Province Boycott Exams 203

The Entire Class of General Third Grade, Group A, Ordered to Leave School

Anqing Correspondence: Recently, public and private schools in Anhui, due to the impending winter vacation, have been holding semester exams one after another. At the Provincial Senior High School, the students of Group A of the third grade of the general course, on the afternoon of the 16th, during the Western History exam given by teacher Weng, were nowhere to be found in the classroom. They had also written insulting words about Weng on the blackboard in the classroom before leaving the school as a group. Principal Sun Wenyuan reported everything to the Department of Education. Zheng Hechun, the acting secretary of the Department of Education, instructed him to handle the matter carefully. Later, Governor Liu Zhenhua of the province heard about it and notified the Department of Education by phone that evening to send the semester exam schedule for all secondary schools in the provincial capital for review, and instructed them to investigate separately. The Department of Education immediately sent it to the Provincial Government overnight. Then, Mr. Sun reported to the Department of Education that the students of Group A of the third grade of the general course had boycotted the exam. After guiding them, they still showed no remorse and proposed a handling method: (1) Order them to leave school immediately; (2) Before the start of the next semester, wait for the school's screening notice to return to school and take a make-up exam. Secretary Zheng and Principal Sun went to the Provincial Government, and Mr. Liu personally approved the words "order to leave school" on the original report and instructed them to comply immediately. The Department of Education immediately transferred the order to comply. On the morning of the 17th at 7:00 a.m., Mr. Liu came to the school, and Secretary Zheng of the Department of Education also went there at 7:00 a.m. Immediately, he supervised Principal Sun and ordered the entire class of Group A of the third grade of the school to leave school and return to their hometowns at 11:00 a.m. The students of that class immediately obeyed the order and left school at 10:00 a.m. to return to their hometowns. The other classes continued to take the exam as usual. (January 19)

Starting at 7:30 PM in the West Qing Gymnasium

8:20 PM, Xinyang vs. Mingqiang Final

Although Nanxing's strong players were scattered, all the players were united and persisted in fighting, closely following behind. The first half ended temporarily with 18 to 13. In the second half, Youbang worked harder. The three forwards cooperated and scored a lot. Finally, Nanxing hoped to draw, but it was still defeated with 32 to 49 due to its inability to resist.

Hong Kong's Official Football Lineup for the Inter-Port Tournament 224

Free Talk

Slaughterhouse 235

— Shi Heng

I heard that there is a large-scale slaughterhouse in Chicago, USA. The most shocking thing is a huge cow-killing machine, which I can't even imagine what kind of device it is. It is said that every day, groups of cows, dozens or hundreds of them, are driven into the machine alive, and when they come out from the other side, there are no more live cows. The cowhide, cow bones, and beef are separated cleanly.

I often imagine this magical machine, and I always feel that it is symbolic.

Casually flipping through the daily newspapers, we can always see that, like that machine killing cows, this modern devil-like big city has slaughtered countless human lives. Just like the cows being driven into that terrible big machine, countless hungry humans from economically bankrupt rural areas or areas that have become famine-stricken due to drought and flood disasters are driven into this murderous city.

But they are not like cows, who are prepared to be slaughtered, to have their lives taken away, and to have their skin, bones, flesh, and blood separated. They are asking for life, asking for a job to live! However, the only way out that this city has prepared for them is to endure hunger and cold, beg on the streets, and wait for that final death. If they are brave, after a burst of angry roar, they can take their lives as a transaction, better as petty thieves and burglars, and even more vicious as robbers and kidnappers. If they can survive for a while, they are lucky. If something happens, it is no worse than those who have already died on the road. There are also those who are weaker and do not even have access to evil. They really become cows, taking their wives and children and throwing themselves into the Huangpu River, or first killing their loved ones with their own hands, and then committing suicide.

We often hear and see these things, and we don't feel anything. It is less surprising than someone telling us about that huge machine in Chicago that kills cows because this city is much larger. It is not as concrete as when we imagine that machine killing cows. However, can we say that this modern city is not more terrible than that machine that kills cows every day?

A Brief Discussion on Literature and Art 236

— Yu Shixia

In the past, Wang Shizhen once made nine lives for articles: First, poverty; second, suspicion and jealousy; third, blemishes and defects; fourth, frustration; fifth, exile; sixth, punishment and humiliation; seventh, premature death; eighth, incompleteness; ninth, no descendants. Later, he added malignant diseases, making a total of ten lives. Articles have ten major sins against people. People are inherently innocent, and the sin lies in the articles. Those who have a pen must be aware of this!

I now announce the crimes of literature and art. I will only list the major aspects. In short, there are three crimes:

Scholars should first have the capacity for learning and insight, and then literature and art. Once one becomes a writer, one is no longer worthy of respect. If a person is useless, literature and art are to blame. This is the first major crime of literature and art.

Virtue is the root, and literature and art are the branch. If one has surplus energy after practicing virtue, then one can study literature. If a person has no virtue, literature and art are to blame. This is the second major crime of literature and art.

Yan Zhitui said that the essence of writing is to highlight interest and express the spirit, which makes people arrogant and conceited, so they neglect self-cultivation and are eager to make progress. Today's literati are particularly troubled by this. Once they have a satisfactory matter or a clear sentence, their spirit soars to the clouds and their ambition surpasses the ages. They sing and appreciate themselves, unaware that there are others around. If a person invites disaster, literature and art are to blame. This is the third major crime of literature and art.

I have enumerated the crimes of literature and art, and it is complete with three. Flipping through the news, I add another crime. What is the crime? It hinders mathematics. Expanding on this, it endangers science. Classical Chinese is gone, and vernacular has taken its place. I excerpt the words of a certain gentleman as follows:

...Chinese people have always disliked numbers. Vague adverbs such as "probably" and "approximately" are often the buzzwords of Chinese people. Most middle school students tend to dislike mathematics because the temptation of literary books often uses "incompatibility" as a reason to erase mathematics with one stroke. This is really a dangerous thing. Today's science is built on mathematics. Academic disciplines that are entered into by mathematics can be accurately established as science. For example, when mathematics enters the realm of astronomy, astronomy becomes an accurate science. The same is true for other physics, chemistry, psychology, economics, etc. In recent years, in the entrance examinations for freshmen in various universities, out of a thousand math test papers, about 500 have received a zero score. With the level of mathematics being so low, what are we talking about scientific research?

The words of a certain gentleman are insightful and incisive. If it were not for the temptation of literary books, why would middle school students be unwilling to study mathematics deeply? If the level of mathematics were not so low, why would China have no scientific research to speak of? With this in mind, China's failure to progress in science, leading to cultural backwardness and national misfortune, is originally the sin of literature and art. Alas, literature and art, your sins are indeed countless!

Guest 237

— Dao Wu

A guest came this day.

The wife opened the door and, seeing that a guest had arrived, hurriedly called out loudly:

"Jianhu, Aunt and Sister-in-law are here!" It seemed as if she was warning him. This warning indeed shook him and gave him a big fright.

So the husband came out to greet them, and the two of them, while busying themselves to invite these two honored guests to sit down, secretly looked at each other, each understanding the other's thoughts. However, they had no choice but to ask each other tentatively: What should we do?

These two guests were very distinguished. One was the wife's aunt, and the other was this aunt's new daughter-in-law. The aunt didn't come often, and her new daughter-in-law was visiting for the first time. After the aunt settled down, she said, "The daughter-in-law hasn't been out much since she joined the family. I thought I'd take her around to visit some relatives while the weather is nice, so everyone can see each other more often in the future. Today, we're visiting you first. Because you are the furthest away, it's not easy to come."

She explained her intention, and the hosts quickly echoed, expressing their welcome. The husband called to his wife, "Quick, bring some refreshments."

The wife readily agreed, but her eyes were fixed on him, as if asking, "Where are the refreshments?" So she told her husband to quickly boil water. And since Aunt smokes, bring a pack of cigarettes as well.

The two hurried back inside. The wife complained to her husband, "What about the refreshments? There's no rice at home, what refreshments can we offer?"

The husband held the kettle in one hand and extended the other to her, softly saying, "The copper coins left over from last night are enough to buy water. But what about the money for cigarettes?" He seemed to be retaliating against her. But what to do? He couldn't think of a solution.

The wife took out two jiao (small coins) from under the pillow and handed them to him, "Quick, go buy some refreshments." He took them, put down the kettle, and ran out the back door. Soon, he returned with several paper parcels, panting. The wife was just bringing in glass cups and saucers from outside. The guest outside said loudly, "Don't bother. We'll be coming often in the future, there's no need to be so polite."

The wife replied while asking her husband, "What to do?" The husband frowned, shaking his head anxiously, and replied, "These are all your relatives, what can I do?"

The wife got angry, and the two almost started arguing. But then, they both seemed to be awakened by something. The wife went out with two plates filled with refreshments, and the husband stood there in a daze, thinking that they had passed the first hurdle. Now, how to get through the second one?

The wife came back with a smile, but then her face turned bitter. The husband asked, "Now, we should buy a pack of cigarettes, is there still money?"

The wife asked in surprise, "You haven't bought the cigarettes yet? Why didn't you buy them at the same time?"

He was reminded by her that he had indeed miscalculated, but replied, "Buying all the refreshments wasn't enough, how could I have money left over to buy cigarettes?"

She was stunned, then suddenly remembered something. She quickly opened the wardrobe, took out a newly made qipao that she hadn't worn yet, and threw it to him.

"Is there anything else? You haven't even worn this one yet."

"Hurry up, what does it matter whether it's been worn or not?" The wife almost shouted. The husband turned around, picked up the kettle, and went out. He had no time to hesitate.

After visiting two or three pawnshops, the pawnshop assistants seemed to be deliberately making things difficult for him. Finally, he shouted angrily, "Do whatever you want, just pawn it! This is a new qipao that hasn't been worn, you see." He painfully took it back and handed it over again…

He returned with a pawn ticket and two banknotes, feeling much relieved. Later, they kept the guests for a meal. Both the husband and wife treated the guests very satisfactorily, looking at each other from time to time, conveying their mutual comfort. After the meal, the wife accompanied the aunt and new sister-in-law to chat, and the husband paced back and forth in the room with peace of mind. The topic suddenly turned to playing mahjong. The aunt liked to play mahjong. She casually suggested:

"How about we play a few rounds today?"

They were almost stunned. The wife looked at her husband, silent. He pretended to be very calm, echoing repeatedly, while calculating in his heart how he only had two or three double haos left. He urged his wife to invite the landlady to join, or he could avoid getting involved by acting a role and escaping this difficult situation.

The wife indeed invited the landlady and brought the mahjong tiles. After the introductions, they arranged the table and chairs. The aunt and the landlady sat down first, leaving two places empty on either side. The husband knew he couldn't escape and sat down. The wife insisted on pulling the new sister-in-law to sit down, but the new sister-in-law declined modestly, saying "I don't know how," so the two started pushing back and forth, and the dispute was not easily resolved.

As a result of the argument, the aunt decided that the new daughter-in-law should play. She knew that her niece still had to entertain the guests and manage things, so she couldn't play. This decision was made after her careful and considerate consideration.

The game continued until dark. After dinner, according to the aunt's wishes, they had to continue playing, but fortunately the new sister-in-law had to leave.

Calculating the wins and losses, the husband lost, owing the new sister-in-law more than two yuan. What to do? He asked his wife, "Do you have any money on you? Give it to me." He knew she didn't have any, but he couldn't help but ask.

Unexpectedly, the wife took out two banknotes and gave them to him. So it ended without difficulty. The guests casually took the money, said goodbye, and they saw them to the street corner.

After returning, the husband breathed a long sigh of relief, then suddenly remembered something and asked with a smile, "Where did the two banknotes come from just now?" The wife smiled bitterly and pointed to the bed with her mouth. He looked and saw that a quilt was missing. He sighed, and the two could only smile bitterly at each other.

The Question of Muslims Not Eating Pork (Continued) 238

— Ma Yiyuan

The second time was a conversation with an Egyptian student supervisor stationed in Lyon. His explanation was as follows:

"The Koran is for all ages, so in the days when science was not developed, Allah had forbidden us to eat pork. Now that modern science has developed, the slaughterhouses in cities like Berlin, Germany, although they do not prohibit eating pork, their inspections are particularly strict!

Berlin slaughters about thousands of pigs every day. The slaughterhouse has a special inspection room, divided into two parts, each with fifteen people. During slaughter, a piece is cut from the left and right kidneys of each pig, numbered, and then sent to this room for separate inspection. Only after being verified as non-toxic can it be sold. Because there is a microorganism called trichina (trichinella) parasitic in the pig's body that can make people sick. So I think that the Muslim prohibition of eating pork is entirely for hygiene reasons. As for touching it, I have not seen any explicit prohibition. But if it is filthy all over, it is not a pig, we would not want to get close to it.

Like raising pigs for profit, I think it is wrong, and it is considered a violation of religious tenets. But the extreme avoidance of pigs and pork by the Muslims in your country, and even the tea offered by people of other religions is not accepted, is a bit of an overcorrection."

The third time was a visit to three Arabs in the Qingzhen (mosque) in Paris, which was built in recent years. They are all "Ahmadi" (i.e., long education). After I raised the question, they made the following explanations:

"The Koran forbids us to eat pork, so we should not eat it. It is wrong to use hygiene reasons or the knowledge of science to justify it. We need to be clean. Since pigs are dirty, of course we don't need to touch them on purpose. Meat with bloodstains, not just pork, is enough to stain our clothes. It is enough to wash it clean. The classic only prohibits eating, there is no other basis." "If someone says that soap is made of lard, can Muslims not use it?" I asked again.

"It is not said that soap is absolutely not made of lard, even if it is made of lard, as long as you use it to remove dirt, you can use it, because we only prohibit 'eating' pork." "Can a toothbrush made of pig bristles be used by Muslims to brush their teeth in their mouths?"

"Yes, because you only use it to brush your teeth, and the scripture prohibits 'eating pork.' You only need to be faithful to the prohibition of the scripture." "Someone once asked a great scholar, if a calf is raised on pig milk, can this calf be eaten by Muslims? He replied that it can, because the cow is still a cow and has not become a prohibited animal, so it can be eaten. My religion is very free and very generous. Just look at this explanation to know what the spirit of my religion is like."

In summary, the above three conversations prove that my grandfather's claim is indeed reasonable. In addition to "not eating pork," all kinds of dietary taboos of Muslims in our country are enough to increase the estrangement with people of other religions, and restrict the development of Muslim professions, leading to an added layer of hardship in the lives of the Muslim masses. I hope that this article can help them consider, on a stand that does not violate religious teachings, to improve their habits, so that it may not be without some benefit to communicating common feelings and expanding the scope of Muslim professions. (The End)

Father and Daughter (4) 239

— Jin Yi

As he spoke, he inserted his fingers into her hair and stroked it. His trembling hands made her hair hurt. But she tried to endure it and didn't dare say anything.

She watched her father put on his pajamas and lie down on the bed. She personally arranged the mosquito net neatly. Then, saying goodnight, she gently walked out and returned to her bedroom.

That night, there was good moonlight, which shone through the window screen and cast the flowers on the screen onto the floor. She lay on the bed, quietly listening to the complete silence of the entire world. She thought of the mother she had never met, sketching her in her mind, and gradually fell asleep. That night, she had dreams one after another, and in those dreams, the father's face flashed. She woke up before dawn and walked to her father's bedroom. When she pushed open the door, and opened it only enough for one person to pass through, she was blocked by something. She didn't push hard, flattened her body, and barely squeezed in. She immediately saw her father sleeping on the floor at the door, with saliva flowing from the corner of his mouth, and two empty wine bottles lying beside him.

Suddenly, she began to cry. She felt that he was not her father, but just an evil person. The sadness accumulated in her chest poured out, and she fell on the bed and cried loudly.

The sound of crying woke the father who was sleeping on the ground. He woke up, raised his eyes, saw her, shook his head in shame, and struggled to support himself with his arms. He sighed a long sigh, and because he had no strength, he lay back on the ground.

Hearing his sigh, the daughter suppressed her grief, stopped crying, raised her face from her palms, saw his pitiful appearance, and naturally stood up, sobbing, walked to where he was lying, bent down and helped him up, and let him sit on the low chair with a back. She herself went to the bedside and sat down.

He sat there, silently, without a sound. Tears gradually formed in his eyes, slowly becoming bigger and bigger, and then flowed down his cheeks. His face was twisted in pain, as if he had something to say but couldn't, and his tears flowed down even more.

"Dad, you don't love me, you don't love me!"

She murmured, her face was plain, with no expression at all. It seemed that there was no need to worry too much about such a father, and there was no need to care about him.

Financial and Gold Markets Remain Stable, Hovering Around 90 Yuan 240

Silver Price and Exchange Rate Continue to Fall, Resulting in a Rise of Two Yuan

The gold market was quite stable yesterday, hovering around 90 yuan all day. Public sentiment is still stable and the underlying momentum is also good. In the early morning, overseas silver markets in the UK and the US both fell, with forward silver prices on the Gold and Silver Exchange falling by 1.1 to 2%. Exchange rates were uniformly lower. London gold fell by 1 penny, US cotton fell by 8 points, US wheat fell by 0.75, and stock fluctuations were minimal. The wool market opened with an initial call of 87.8 yuan, public sentiment was quite good, and major players were also interested in buying, gradually rising to 93.4 yuan, and then slightly declining. The market was flat at the beginning of the opening, but the domestic market was loose and abundant, and silver companies were selling, causing the gold price to fall below 90 yuan. The determination of the industry was still firm, so there were still many rebounds, but Western merchants such as Sassoon and George & Co. still had a desire to sell, and at noon it was still within 90 yuan. The afternoon market was quite calm, with supply and demand in the market balanced, forming a spiral. When Reuters reported that the US would find ways to implement its gold policy, but would prevent future silver imports, the industry initially thought it would benefit silver prices and selling increased sharply. But after the full text was typed out, after careful reading, it had no impact on silver prices. Repeated buying then returned to stability, retail shorts made up for their positions, and the market closed above 90 yuan. After the market closed, rumors spread that the US was planning to purchase silver, and finally retreated to within 90 yuan. The settlement price was 1,090 yuan. The daily market situation is recorded below.

The opening price in the morning was 691 yuan 9 jiao, up 2 yuan 6 jiao from last Saturday. Goods opened at 2 yuan 2 jiao. The exchange market opened with a recent selling price of 1 shilling 4 pence 3125 for British exchange and 34 yuan for US exchange. Hengyu made progress, but because the Zhengjin Huabisai March US dollar was 25, it gradually moved downstream from 2 yuan 8 jiao. It was expected that HSBC's listing price would not move. Hengxing, Yuanmao, Yongda, Decheng and others sold together. Silver companies sold Zhengjin's January US dollar 1.875 and May 8.125, and fell to within 89 yuan. Dafa, Yongbing and Xingna made some struggles, and when Shanghai came out with May US dollar 875, Hengxing, Daxing and Yong sold again, and fell to 87 yuan 6 jiao. Shenkang took advantage of the low price to enter, and gradually rebounded. After entering, May US dollar 875 was difficult to settle. Zhifeng, Yongyi, Fengyong, Daxing, Yongzhaofeng and Changyuanmao bought together, and rose to 90 yuan 2 jiao. Silk and Tea: Chinese and Foreign Silk Markets Both Fall into Silence 259

(US Raw Silk Imports Decrease) The United States does not produce silk, but its consumption of raw silk is greater than that of any other country in the world. It relies entirely on silk-producing countries such as China, Japan, Italy, and France to supply it. Its raw silk imports amount to about 600,000 bales per year. In recent years, due to the impact of artificial silk dumping, raw silk imports have gradually decreased. In the past year, total raw silk imports from various countries were only 503,376 bales, a decrease of 84,537 bales compared to the previous year.

(Wuxi Factory Shipments to Shanghai Are Scarce) Since the beginning of the year, few silk factories in Wuxi have started work, and silk production has decreased daily. The number of January futures silk sold by various manufacturers in Shanghai is limited. In the blink of an eye, the end-of-month silk delivery period is approaching, but shipments to Shanghai are scarce. In the past few days, a total of only 54 bales of white factory warp such as Moon Rabbit and Double Eagle brands have been shipped.

(Artificial Silk Sales Are Still Active) Mainland silk thread merchants' imports of artificial silk are still active. Yesterday, 15 boxes of Hong Yutou No. 1 brand were imported from Yanqing and other groups, priced at 228.75 yuan, 20 boxes of No. 2, priced at 202.5 yuan, and 12 boxes of Golden Dragon brand, priced at 211.75 yuan net.

(Chinese and Foreign Silk Merchants Take Advantage of Cheap Prices to Replenish Stocks) European and American silk thread merchants still have thick stocks of silk in hand, but consumption is still decreasing. Chinese silk prices are high, and no one asks about them. Silk reports are still rarely transferred to Shanghai. Various European firms and mainland silk merchants in this port, in view of the fact that silk prices have fallen to the lowest limit, are taking advantage of cheap prices to replenish their shortages. A total of 15 bales of yellow and white factory warp, 30 bales of gray warp, and 5 bales of yellow silk were traded, and prices remained firm.

Page 17

Supplement of Shanghai News

Talk

The day before yesterday, the funeral of Admiral Du Xigui took place. On the routes it passed, there were many roadside memorials. The viewers were as numerous as mountains and seas, all craning their necks and standing on tiptoe, wanting to feast their eyes.

By the time the funeral procession passed, the ceremony was very simple, with only a few military bands. It was not as extravagant as Sheng Xingsheng's funeral, and the viewers were greatly disappointed.

I wonder why Du Xigui didn't earn a few more dollars during his lifetime, so that he could display more "Huarong Road" during his funeral, allowing passersby to watch to their hearts' content.

Nowadays, people from all walks of life, especially traitors and treacherous merchants, are desperately making money, regardless of everything. Could it be for such a reason? However, the government has already issued a strict ban on the ceremonies of the former Qing Dynasty.

Watching a Play 270

— Mei

"Let's not talk about national affairs, let's just talk about romance." Writers in 1934 seemed to have this trend. In fact, what is there to talk about in national affairs in this year? So, leaving aside national affairs, let's talk about plays!

It is said that the most popular actors now, who can easily make money, are female roles specializing in playing virtuous and refined women and lively, flirtatious women – what we usually call huadan. Generally, the huadan appears in the last act, which is colloquially called the "closing play." Anyone who performs the "closing play" must have both beauty and talent, as well as great skills and magic, to be qualified. Otherwise, before the end of the show, the audience in the audience will all leave, which would be a great disappointment. Therefore, although there are distinctions among stage actors now, such as dignified male roles, painted-face roles, martial male roles, and clowns, the headliners who earn the big money are mostly huadan.

Although the number of unemployed people in the city is increasing in batches, entertainment venues are also increasing day by day. If you ask why, only the Great Stage across the street knows; but on the other hand, it can truly reflect the national character of the Great Republic of China – one can skip eating, but one cannot skip watching plays. Since the January 28th Incident in Shanghai, the city's economy has been deteriorating, plummeting sharply. Although the old shops have been using the gimmick of "big discounts" to attract ordinary citizens with weak purchasing power, the year-end accounts always show debts exceeding assets. As a result, some are laying off employees and cutting salaries, while others have to close down. Logically, with such a depressed economy, people should have long disappeared from entertainment venues! But now, it's the exact opposite!

But then again! The people of Shanghai are indeed blessed. As long as my father has money, I can watch my play, so why should I care what you say!

The second plate seems like the host mistakenly added ginger, so even he has to sigh; but it doesn't feel too strange. The third plate doesn't skimp on using chili peppers. The students have tender mouths and soft tongues after all, so it's no wonder they hurriedly decline politely, right?

### To a Friend ×× 272

— Mai Fu

| Love and Marriage |

It's been a while since I last saw you. I hope you're living well. As for me, thank goodness, my life is still the same as before, except that I have a few more cigarette tins and a big pile of worries.

Originally, my life was quite leisurely; it's just that the devil disturbed people and insisted on giving me a share of peace and happiness, sending me a little bit of trouble, which made me, who is lazy to speak, pick up a Western pen and spill words to you.

Alas, my friend, how could you not know about my love story? Li loves me. This comes so frankly and naturally, but there are detours, and I am forced to take them.

You know, I've always been very strange. I believe that as long as the other person truly loves me, there's no need for a third party to ask about it. I treat her as a friend, as a mistress, as long as she's willing. Haven't those who have children already gone through this before? Just because they have children, can they put on a stinking act?

The matter is like this, telling it will also make you angry! A few days ago, I wanted Li to come out and chat with me, and I missed the appointment. Then, I telegraphed her again, but she surprisingly didn't come, making chatting impossible and leading to叹天 (嘆天, sighing to the heavens). The day after the telegram, she came slowly. As soon as she met me, she burst into tears in my arms. Crying and telling me, she said that her father knew she loved me, and knew that I loved her, and also knew that we loved each other very deeply. So he insisted on interrupting us, and wouldn't allow Li to see me unless we got engaged.

Friend, look at how ridiculous this guy is!

You know, I never accept that kind of restraint, saying that I love her and am willing to sacrifice anything for her is okay, even if she lives with me, and then we separate after living together, and after separating you want me to sacrifice, I nearly have nothing to say. But forcing me to put on shackles is something I wouldn't do even if I were beheaded. Her father wants an engagement, wants marriage, just wanting to use a fake ceremony to bind me. He wants to keep me alive as a prisoner, guarding her to the death. Don't you think this is so ridiculous, underestimating me like this.

Think about it: engagement and marriage are such ridiculous games, how could someone's love, or lack thereof, be arranged so simply by you? If I didn't love her anymore, would the marriage ceremony stop me from avoiding divorce? Just because a ring isn't exchanged, you think we won't stay together for a thousand years? Really ridiculous, ridiculous! Nonsense, nonsense!

Friend, I am completely against marriage. I think coming up with this kind of thing is simply a conspiracy of love! Since it is a union of love, it must be maintained by love. If you want to maintain this union of love with ugly clauses, then come, but煩惱 (troubles) are煩惱 (troubles), and after all, the idea is the idea! You must know that I will not submit!

Li may disregard her father. She said she would come to live with me in three days. Whether she comes or not is still unknown, but I'll use this to test her, to see if she is easy to get but not easy to let go.

If writing so seriously only makes you laugh, then I really have to curse you as a bastard.

Whether you reply or not, it's up to you! Because I don't care whether you come or not. Goodbye.

Family Letter 273

— Mu

Today I received a letter from my father. Regarding what I said in my previous letter about making a living by writing in Shanghai and only being able to support myself, and not relying on the family too much, my father said in his letter, "What you said about not relying on the family too much makes me want to cry! Although I have many children, they are all selfish and I can't help it. None of them have your talent and qualifications. What they earn is not enough, so it's difficult to take care of the family; and I regret that your father has no talent or virtue to move my children. The old father, young brothers, and sisters at home can hardly survive even on thin porridge. You, as the eldest brother, should be a role model for your brothers; that is the only reasonable thing to do." I also received a letter from my fourth brother saying, "My illness is getting worse and worse. My blood vessels are getting more and more blocked. I can't walk more than a few steps. The other person can't hear clearly when I speak. In the classroom, the elementary school students sitting in the back row often say they can't hear me. What should I do? There is less than a month left before the holidays. Now I can only try my best to persevere. I will try to recuperate next year. But with such financial difficulties, even if I want to recuperate, I won't be able to. I'll just have to listen and let it go. It would be better to finish my debts!"

In ancient times, because of inconvenient transportation, distant mountains, and the chaos of war, there was a saying that "a family letter is worth ten thousand gold." Now that I have received this "ten thousand gold" family letter, although I also feel that it is enough to comfort my feelings, how can I not be worried and sad when the family letter is so full of tears!

After reading the family letter, I was stunned for a long time. I was already saddened by my aging father's plight in his later years, let alone the fact that he still has to maintain a family of more than a dozen people in a declining urban household to feed. He has never enjoyed life. When he was doing business, he was racking his brains to maintain a situation that was about to go bankrupt. He doesn't understand what entertainment is, and he doesn't understand what leisure is. He only knows how to find ways to maintain his business. After the family went bankrupt, he only knew how to save money and maintain the family's life, and how to find ways to get his younger siblings into school to seek knowledge... He is now with white hair and white beard, still trying to find money to feed a family of more than a dozen people and buy supplies for his younger siblings to go to school. What he hopes for is that his grown-up sons will send money home to take care of the family, but other than the fourth and seventh brothers, the sixth and eighth brothers are unemployed, and I, in this big city with more people than jobs, make a living by selling articles and can only support myself! Father, there are many declining urban families who cannot maintain their lives! Since the collapse of the rural economy, haven't the peasant families living in the countryside also been equally poor? We are a part of the poor people in China. We are neither workers nor peasants. Our declining urban family is the petty bourgeoisie. The times and classes have no way to reverse our tragic fate!…

What the family relies on is our grown-up sons. The fourth brother is teaching while ill. The seventh brother wrote from Nanyang saying that he was spitting blood due to overwork in stone printing and painting and may have to be laid off. Why do these two brothers have to get sick? The fourth brother said in his letter, "It would be better to finish my debts." I thought of the third, fifth, and second younger siblings who died young. They once made me cry at that time. Now that I think about it, they died early and are not responsible for the family or society. They are happier! We cannot seek death now. We must continue to fight for life and fulfill our obligations as human beings. We dare not hope for happiness. We have to grit our teeth and face suffering. That is life!

Mr. Miao Chongqun said at the end of "The Barefoot Person" published in "Free Talk," "Death is quite solemn in itself, right? But I think it's okay to shout like that: (the coffin carriers shout in mourning, congratulations,) they shout 'mourning,' and then 'congratulations.' It seems that a person's two-sided meanings are all there. When life walks the road to death, although in one sense it is mournful, in another sense it is also congratulatory! However, we - father, oh brothers - with the obligations of this family of more than a dozen people waiting to be fed on our shoulders, what is there to congratulate about death for us except for mournfulness? There is also the obligation that the social class gives us - we also need to fulfill our responsibilities. If we die, it is selfish, and congratulations are selfish!

If life is only for oneself, it is like the hedonist's drunken dream of life and death, which is inevitably boring. A life without ideals - the ideal of creating happiness for society and humanity, not simply the ideal of enjoying oneself - is difficult for anyone to endure, right? However, the blessed mediocre people live day after day without ideals, which causes those with brains, knowledge, and thoughts to have difficult questions to answer. To have an ideal life means that you have already ridden on the back of a tiger and have to whip the tiger forward! Since you are unwilling to live a mediocre life without ideals, then you have no choice but to grit your teeth, face the pain, and fight on. Life is like this, and this is life.

Reading family letters and rambling thoughts gave me the above life philosophy.

Brother Mao and Sister Bao Travel the World 274

— Meng

Profession and Career 275

— Mai Fu

People generally think that profession is the same as career, and career is the same as profession. There is no difference between them, at most they are just two names for the same thing. If our ancestors had said these words and left them behind, it would not be inaccurate; but if we talk about those surviving in today's society, there can't be no flaws.

We know that a profession is a job for a person to make a living. This business does not arise from one's own feelings, but is determined by an unknowable social force. A career, on the other hand, is a person's ambition, a person's desire, a person's attempt to express his strong life consciousness and launch a　人生(life)　　大(great)　企图(attempt).

If we carefully observe the current society, we will at least feel that it is not the society we need. Because it is full of contradictions, full

Page 19

of mistakes, full of unspeakable chaos and inversion. Everywhere there are contradictions and the opposition of contradictions. Looking from our own standpoint, everything is pitch black.

Naturally, in such a society, we are not allowed to do what we want to do. We have to suffer social obstacles everywhere. Life dictates that we spend most of our time engaged in the war for bread. No matter how enthusiastic you are about dedicating yourself to literature or art, in order to hunt for daily bread, you have to restrain your enthusiasm and find a job that you don't want but can provide bread to feed your life. The current society does not allow career and profession to be combined into one. It does not allow you to want to be an artist, and only give you a share of bread based on your identity as an artist. Therefore, in this defective society, we must separate career and profession - career is one thing, and profession is another.

Because a profession is not the work we want, in order to satisfy a desire in our hearts - the desire to express our will to human society through our life activities, we must act according to our personality. For example, I want to become an inventor, or an artist, or a pivotal figure in politics in an era. These scientific and artistic researches, and political activities, are my heart's desires, and are the expression of my will. When these desires are not completely satisfied, it means that my career has not succeeded. We have to rely on something that is completely against our will to sustain our research.

This arduous struggle is the great spirit of mankind, and it is also the place of greatness in our humanity. In us, we should stimulate the development of this spirit. The stimulation of this spirit is a kind of promotion of human society, and it is also an expectation of the arrival of the society we hope for.

Therefore, no matter what, we must separate career and profession. Because if we treat career as a profession and confuse them, we will make the mistake of not fully understanding the current society. As a result, because a profession cannot meet the desires of a career, we will inevitably develop life's suffering. If we treat a profession as a career and confuse them, the result will be that because a profession is a completely meaningless job, we will end up just "living in vain." It will completely engulf our hearts, engulf our wills, and the activity of our life consciousness will only be an unconscious mass. If we can distinguish clearly that a career is a career and a profession is a profession, then we should have an assessment of the career, a resolve to prepare and engage in the struggle. And for the profession, we will neither feel that it is empty, nor will we feel that it is boring and meaningless.

The Seven Dollars and Thirty Cents Problem 276

— Yi Ping

Brother Wenbing is really a lovely person. He talked about women for half a day, claiming to be an amateur. Look at the way he described women so naturally. I don't believe that an amateur man knows so much about women. I recently learned that there are positive and negative sides to how you look at articles. Generally speaking, "the ideal woman" is a negative article. If you write a few more "love stories," you will be sent a magnificent high crown. Brother Wenbing, pay attention to the "big gifts" during the big sale era. But all of this is nonsense and has nothing to do with this article. I want to say that "writing articles is nothing more than for the sake of seven dollars and thirty cents" is not a witty remark.

I love literature and art. I have a tree of broken books left to me by my late father. When I have the opportunity to return to my hometown, I will definitely check them in my busy schedule to see if they have been damaged by bookworms, or move them to the yard to sunbathe them. As for the books that I have bought myself, except for those that have disappeared after being borrowed, there are more than enough to set up a used bookstore like a real bookstore: even in this difficult time to live, in the five years I have been in Shanghai, I have a bookshelf full of achievements. However, in the past, as long as there was money in my pocket, I would bring them home regardless of whether they were good or bad; now, the threshold for looking at advertisements is also more refined, and money is naturally less willing to be friends with me than in the past, so most of the works in my small building are above the horizontal line. Wei said that I buy books like "birds bringing food," because I drag them back one by one.

Naturally, at a certain point, I tried to learn to write articles. I believed that everything I wrote was top-notch, so the wastepaper baskets of various newspapers and supplements often had my masterpieces visiting; but I never gave up. I could write today, write tomorrow, write in the morning, write at night. Perhaps the editors of various supplements also forgot to wear their glasses, and they actually passed the dragon gate, and my value increased tenfold, and I arrogantly regarded myself as a writer.

But after all, he is a writer who "regards himself" as such. His works are still produced in large quantities. School publications and school wall newspapers cannot do without his works.

Now I am no longer a financially well-off student, nor am I a writer who "regards himself" as such. Stepping out of the school gate has transformed me, especially the five years of hard life. I don't know anything. When I wake up every day, I remember that I have to eat, my wife has to eat, and my children will also have to beg for food.

In this noodle shop, I think there are enough "writers" in Shanghai to make up the numbers for an aviation 　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　文炳(Wenbing) are you able to admit that the phrase "writing articles is only for seven dollars and thirty cents" is a witty remark? Husband, ah!

I love literature and art, but I never thought that I would rely on this little bit of "leftover heat" of loving literature and art to make a living.

Mandy's Freedom (4) 278

— Mandy

"Are you making fun of me? You don't understand me at all! Heavens, even my friends are finding it hard to deal with me!"

He misunderstood, or perhaps my words were wrong. But his words were truly like a bolt from the blue to me. "You misunderstand. I do understand you. Our lives are indeed playing out a tragedy, but we should use reason to confront our fate. If we let our emotions run wild, we will only become prisoners of fate. What good is that?"

"However, the political environment gives me five parts of stimulation, the social environment gives me five parts of stimulation, and I can't bear it anymore. Now my lover gives me a large portion of stimulation again. What power does my reason have to overcome it? My brain is full of stimulation, my blood vessels are full of stimulation, my whole being will be crushed by this demon of stimulation. If you don't commit suicide, you will be bitten to death by that demon!"

"The stimulation your lover gave you this time was brought on by yourself."

"I brought it on myself?" He stared at me harshly, as if losing his mind.

"Yes," I said, "you brought it on yourself. She once told me that she knew you were living a life of boredom and distress, but you didn't tell her what was causing your boredom and distress. She didn't know what kind of words would truly comfort your heart, so she was living a life of worry and unease. Why do you have to be so proud towards your lover? Why don't you tell her the heartfelt words of your boredom and distress, so she can say words of comfort to you? She doesn't understand you, and you are the one who prevents her from understanding you. How can she live with you?"

"She is dissatisfied with politics! I have discussed politics with her, but she doesn't like to listen; she says it gives her a headache. She is an extreme hedonist! What I love about her is that she has a pure soul, a beautiful body, and the talent to handle matters. What does it matter if she dislikes politics? Unexpectedly, unexpectedly, it has led to mutual pain! She doesn't understand political thought, therefore she doesn't understand the distress I get from political thought. And I, I don't want her to understand political thought, so as not to engrave indelible and unavoidable scars on her pure soul. Thus, just like that, good in worry and unease, I am in boredom and distress... it turns out it's my fault! But, it's not that I don't let her understand me, it's because I love her that I don't want her to taste the cup of bitterness! And she, she doesn't understand my love, she left me, she's gone! Alas!"

After that, he went to your house, but you didn't see him, and you left Shanghai for a distant place. Why didn't you even see him? Now he is even more "abnormal". In the lecture hall, he talks to students about "literature" but elaborately tells the story of Flaubert's "Madame Bovary" to discuss women's psychology, and nitpicks on the story of Ibsen's play "Nora" to discuss women's character. His conclusion is the same as that of Christians, teaching students that it's best not to marry or fall in love with women. Look, is he an ascetic? No. He is reacting against women because of heartbreak!

He is drinking even more now, at least five or six bottles each time, not stopping until he is drunk. Once he is drunk, all sorts of shocking complaints pour out of his mouth like a torrent. He speaks frankly about his dissatisfaction with politics, his hatred for society, and the misdeeds of so-and-so. He is a person who has lost his heart!
