Director Aspects of "Dinner Party": Shi Dongshan, Ying Yunwei

"Dinner Party" has excited many Shanghai movie fans because of its list of eight famous stars. As in other countries, it has also won a lot of praise, and it seems to be a rare treasure in the film industry. Precisely because it is so valued, precisely because it has a higher evaluation, then, people who go to appreciate it with great hope may be disappointed to some extent.

The director of "Dinner Party" is George Cukor (G. Gukor), who is considered a prestigious artist in Hollywood. His "War and Chastity" and "David Copperfield" have always left a deep impression on people.

From an artistic point of view, his works, from the title to the color of the play, have his own achievements. After sound films completely seized the film market, old writers fell one after another, but Cukor went from stage to screen and became an achiever among new artists.

Regarding his style, generally speaking, his works are very clear and also have a free and easy style. In some cases, it is similar to W. Dedare's works. His works are loved by general adults, especially intellectuals in the city, who are more easily moved by his works. Conversely, people who like Tom Mix and the like are definitely not understanders of his works. In his works, there are few Speedy Climaxes, but his clear spring-like fluent technique is very refined and brisk, but it does not flow into frivolity. Therefore, in the hearts of happy people, a certain bright Touch is left for a long time, overflowing with a clear and happy mood. In "Dinner Party", we will not ignore these advantages either, that is to say, his special technique is still clearly unfolding.

However, in "Dinner Party", we cannot agree that he cannot eliminate the stage techniques, dividing a play into several paragraphs, although using chimes to explain the passage of time, the explanation of time is always unclear. In fact, many people think that these are not events that happened in one day.

Of course, we don't say that we forgive his stage skills because he was originally a stage person, but the main reason is that since so many big stars are suddenly put together, each big star must have the opportunity to perform. Therefore, in order to distribute them relatively evenly, in order to make positions for a large number of stars to express themselves, it has almost formed a variety show-style performance for each.

Furthermore, if people think that this is something with great significance, and that these few stars are needed to perform from an artistic point of view, then we will never ignore the great spirit of American films. However, the fact is not like this. Obviously, it is the entrepreneurs who are trying to make a final struggle, and trying to use the names of big stars to call on a large number of movie fans.

Since the motive of the producer is like this, and the short-sighted vision is only focused on a large amount of money, then we feel that this injection for neurasthenia is a bit ridiculous. And from an artistic point of view, one cannot help but sigh because of it.

Indeed, after the luxurious banquet of "Dinner Party", the hypocrisy and selfishness of the Americans are exposed, and the collapse of American capitalist society is even more exposed. After we recognize the decisive significance of this, we will not ignore the playwright's frank attitude. From the point of view of the consistent whitewashing of peace by American artists, this attitude is indeed quite commendable.

"Eat, drink, and be merry, for tomorrow we die!" When the group of gentlemen and ladies walked to the dining room, we heard this terrible saying. When they have fallen to the last step, naturally this sentence can intoxicate noble people. But what will the group of small property owners feel, who feel the horror of decline on the one hand, and yearn for the bright future on the other? "Eat, drink, and be merry, for tomorrow we die!" These negative words are precisely the dirge before entering the grave, before the grave. I hope we will cheer up. (This article was written by Ling He, and the previous section was added with my own opinions. It is noted to clarify responsibility.)

Movies and the Countryside 279

— Huang Yingdai

Movies, undoubtedly, are not a purely entertaining tool, and all the pictures on the screen, directly and indirectly, are enough to influence the audience's thoughts and life. In the past, the only purpose of general film companies was business. As long as a film can attract the audience, the material taken, whether it is humble and filthy, and enough to influence the audience, the company does not care about anything. But now, some film companies have realized that the film itself, in addition to providing entertainment, also has the important significance of helping education and improving life, so the style has gradually changed. Recently, a part of the film styles in various countries have paid attention to the trend of the countryside. Indeed, movies and the countryside have a close relationship!

The United States is an advanced country in the film industry. The power of American films occupies the most important position in the world. But we feel that American films in the past had a major drawback, that is, at least nine out of ten films describe urban life. Songs, dances, grand hotels, dance halls, everything is nothing but a microcosm of urban life. However, these decadent urban lives are put on the screen, which is harmful and useless to the audience. But recently, several companies in the United States have changed their style. On the one hand, although they do not completely abandon the depiction of urban life, on the other hand, they pay attention to shooting more films of the current situation in the countryside and the lives of farmers. When the film is screened on the screen, in addition to the depiction of the city, the audience can also see the reality of the countryside. It is not monotonous and boring, and at the same time, it can arouse the audience's interest in rural life and increase their understanding of the current situation in the countryside. In the United States, which is in the revival movement, it is also actively promoting the revival of the agricultural movement, then asking the public to sympathize with the revival of agriculture, the film is naturally an important help, no wonder American film companies want to change their ways and pay attention to films depicting the current situation in the countryside!

Secondly, when we look at Soviet Russia, after the implementation of the New Economic Policy, Soviet Russia vigorously encouraged and promoted the promotion of production. To encourage and promote, film is naturally the best tool, and the use of film by Soviet Russia as a tool for promotion and encouragement is used in another way and another means, which is different from other countries. And what they pay the most attention to is to make films go to the countryside. On the one hand, it has the nature of preaching, and at the same time, it is also instilling agricultural knowledge! The result of preaching, undoubtedly, is to try to make the people of the whole of Russia loyal to the Soviet government; and the result of instilling agricultural knowledge, in the production and economic aspects of Soviet Russia, can naturally get a lot of gains. The method they take is to put the current situation of the countryside and the life of the countryside on the screen and show it in the city, so that people in the city have a deep understanding of everything in the countryside; and on the other hand, they put the application of various new agricultural tools and the achievements of the implementation of collectivized agricultural areas on the film, and use film touring cars to show it in various rural areas, directly and indirectly, can increase the knowledge of farmers. We feel that Soviet Russia's use of film to increase agricultural knowledge is indeed a lot to be learned from.

Recently, in China, the cry of rural bankruptcy has been heard all over the country. But the people in the city are still enjoying themselves and do not know the suffering of the farmers. The film industry must naturally take on the mission of rescuing the countryside, so I think that Chinese film companies should shoot more films about depicting the actual situation in the countryside and the actual life of farmers so that people in the city know that the countryside is bankrupt and the farmers are about to be unable to live. However, we check the facts of the past, and in general, film companies have shot very few films depicting the rural economy and the lives of farmers. Occasionally, a few films take the countryside as the background, but they cannot deeply describe the phenomenon of the countryside. In fact, in China, where capital is very weak and art is very immature, if film companies shoot more films about rural reality, it is not only more meaningful, but also because there is nature as a background, and the clothes of the actors are also rough and simple, and very economical. Then, why don't we shoot more of the rural reality films that are meaningful and economical, and instead shoot films that depict urban life and deformed society?

Snippets of Nanyang Film Industry 280

— Chunlei

The Shanghai film industry is to Nanyang what the Hollywood film industry is to Shanghai, a large sales market. But recently, there has been a slight change, because most of the film companies in Shanghai have been converted to sound films. The dialogue of this sound film is Mandarin, and 99% of the overseas Chinese in Nanyang are Cantonese compatriots, they do not understand Mandarin, naturally their interest in sound films has been reduced a lot.

Therefore, some Cantonese films have emerged in response to the situation, such as "Conscience", "Platinum Dragon", "Broken Heart Monument", "Weeping Flowers", etc., which are quite in line with the taste. However, most of these Cantonese films are adaptations of old stage classical plays, lacking a realistic form and content; moreover, the output is not much, and the supply cannot meet the demand. Under such circumstances, overseas Chinese have the motive to establish film companies. After many preparations, not long ago, a Siam United Film Company was established in Siam.

Last month, when I returned to the south via Hong Kong for business, I watched a premiere of this company's work "Mekong Love Waves" at the Central Grand Theater.

This is a sound film with pure Cantonese dialogue. The content is a love story, and the background is several overseas Chinese men on the banks of the Mekong River: Yuan Shao de and the heroine Hu Jun Shao. Hong Kong has a lot of praise for it. Personally, I think that in addition to the sound recording and photography, which have quite considerable achievements, the consciousness of its content is not very desirable. But since it is a premiere work, a little immaturity is excusable. Moreover, it is the pioneer of Chinese people running artistic enterprises overseas, and its spirit is even more commendable.

This company is located in Bangkok, Siam, and the manager is Li Kunlin. When it was first established, it was supported by local overseas Chinese, the education sector, and the Siamese government. The radio it uses is produced by the American Western Electric Company. It is said that it was purchased with the help of the King of Siam.

Southern and Tianyi Collaborate to Shoot "Singing Stage Love History" 281

— Ji

Xue Juexian of the Southern Company returned to Shanghai last month after being urged by Shao Zuiweng of Tianyi, and continued to cooperate in shooting the second sound film. In addition to his wife Tang Xueqing and his brother-in-law Jueming, Xue also hired Cantonese music masters Yin Zizhong, Chen Shao, Feng Weipei, and Ye Ketian to come with him. However, because Xue's old illness relapsed when he first arrived in Shanghai, and at the same time, the selection of the two plays "Poisonous Rose" and "Hate Not Meeting When Unmarried" was difficult to realize, which delayed the time. It has now been decided to produce the play "Singing Stage Love History" recently written by Xue, which will be directed by Shao Zuiweng. In view of the recent cold weather, Shao specially built another dressing room in the photography field for the film, with perfect heating equipment, for Xue to rest when filming. It is currently under construction day and night, and it is expected to start work in about three or four days, and it is expected to be completed in about a month. (But pay)

Film Novel

BROADWAY　THRU　A　KEYHOLE (3) 282

— Xin Zhi

Roche called Tex over and asked, "Hello, Tex, who is that kid on the edge?" Tex thought he was joking with her, and she said, "I've been wondering about it since you sent her over. But Judge Li Qi wanted to reward her with a bracelet, but she didn't want it and sent the bracelet back. She's also a little fool. You sent her here, don't you even know her name?" Roche looked at the girl carefully again, and suddenly remembered and said, "Oh... that's Qiong Huilan. I said why she doesn't look like someone from your place." Tex sat up straight, with one hand on her hip, and said to Roche, "Mr. Roche, please take care of your reputation." Roche said, "Don't worry about reputation or not, you will send her here when this performance is over!"

After a while, the exquisite and lively Qiong Huilan came. She sat next to Roche, her golden eyes very kindly facing Roche. She said, "Frank, I can't believe it. We haven't seen each other for a long time, and I don't know how many years it has been." Roche smiled at her and said, "Then why don't we have a drink and catch up, okay?" Qiong said: "Thank you, I don't drink. But I want to see you and thank you for all your kindness to me." Roche looked her up and down, with a look of joy on his face, so he asked her to change her clothes and take her to play elsewhere. The play that Roche said was out of the nightclub, and then took her to his own luxuriously decorated apartment. The apartment where the gang lived was originally a very dangerous place. If something happened, there would be no response to shouting. And it is also specially designed for women who nod up and down, but do not shake left and right. Qiong entered Roche's bedroom, and he locked the door behind him. Qiong Lanhu is the first time to a men's apartment, and this is at night, so although she is talking and laughing, she can't help but feel a little uneasy in her heart. She looked around, and the room, in addition to a gramophone, radio, and wine cabinet, also had a double bed.

She took off her coat and sat on the bed unconsciously, unknowingly revealing her curvaceous legs. She was talking about her childhood situation and everything in the nightclub, even the fact that Judge Li Qi sent her a bracelet. Roche took a few kinds of wine from the wine cabinet and mixed them, shook two cocktails, and asked her, "Didn't you say that you returned the bracelet to him later?" Qiong Huilan said, "Of course, I returned it to him." Roche said, "That's okay too." He turned on the radio, took two cocktails, walked to Qiong Huilan's side, and sat on the bed with her, their bodies tightly close together. He handed a cocktail to Qiong Huilan, but Qiong shook her head and said that she never drinks. Roche said, "It doesn't matter if you only drink once. This wine is not fierce either." Qiong said, "If you insist on me drinking it." So they touched their glasses and drank the wine. After a while, Roche asked her if she wanted to drink again. This time Qiong insisted on not drinking anymore. They were still sitting on the bed tightly close together. Roche asked, "Did you really return that bracelet?" Qiong Huilan said, "Of course, how can I take other people's things for nothing without giving them anything in return?" Roche said, "But you have also received my kindness, haven't you?" (To be continued)
